  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function() {
            var form = document.getElementById('search-input');
            form.onsubmit = submitHandler;
        });
        function submitHandler(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            grecaptcha.ready(function() {
                grecaptcha.execute('6Lf1JKUUAAAAADlRmvbTMzYD_fmo83Av-gytnpXw', {action: 'searchSubmission'}).then(function(token) {
                    
                    $('#search-input').prepend('<input type="hidden" name="token" value="' + token + '">');
                    $('#search-input').prepend('<input type="hidden" name="action" value="searchSubmission">');
                    
                    document.getElementById('search-input').submit();
                });
            });
        };
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function showAdvancedHelp() {
            var selectedMethod = $('#searchMethod option:selected').val();
            if (selectedMethod == 'as_is') {
                $('.search-help').css("display","flex");
                $('.exact-phrase').css("display","none");
            }
            else if (selectedMethod == 'exact_phrase') {
                $('.exact-phrase').css("display","flex");
                $('.search-help').css("display","none");
            }
            else {
                $('.exact-phrase').css("display","none");
                $('.search-help').css("display","none");
            }
        }
        function searchOrderByOpen() {
            var item = $('#searchURL').val();
            var searchOrderByPropertyName = getUrlVar(item,'src_orderings[0].propertyName');
            var searchOrderByOperand =  getUrlVar(item,'src_orderings[0].operand');
            if (searchOrderByPropertyName)
            {
                $('#searchOrderOperand').attr('value',searchOrderByOperand);
                if (searchOrderByOperand == 'score') {
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', false);
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', true);
                }
                else {
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('value',searchOrderByPropertyName);
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', true);
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', false);
                }
            }

        }
        function searchOrderByChange() {
                var searchOrderByValue = $('#searchOrderBy').val();
                //alert("no query select value = " + searchOrderByValue);
                if (searchOrderByValue !== 'score') {
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', false);
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', true);

                    $('#searchOrderOperand').val('property');
                }
                else {
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', false);
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', true);
                    $('#searchOrderOperand').val('score');
                }
            //}
        }
        /* The following code, in conjunction with an s:filePath tag can be used to
        provide different collections jnt:file objects based on path

        function checkContentType() {
            var contentType = $('#searchNodeType option:selected').val();
            if (contentType == 'jnt:file') {
                enableFilepath();
            }
            else {
                disableFilepath();
            }
        }
        function disableFilepath() {
            $('#src_filePath_value').attr("name","inactive_src_filePath.value");
            $('#src_pagePath_value').attr("name","src_pagePath.value");
        }
        function enableFilepath() {
            $('#src_filePath_value').attr("name","src_filePath.value");
            $('#src_pagePath_value').attr("name","inactive_src_pagePath.value");
        } */
        function getUrlVar(url,key) {
            var searchURL = unescape(url);
            var searchURLParams = searchURL.split("?");
            var searchURLArray = searchURLParams[1].split("&");
            var keyValue = '';
            jQuery.each(searchURLArray, function(i, value){
                var param = value.split("=")[0];
                if (param == key){
                    keyValue = value.split("=")[1];
                }
            });
            return keyValue;
        }
        function searchNodeTypeChange() {
            var nodeType = $('#searchNodeType option:selected').val();
            if (typeof nodeType == 'undefined') {
                nodeType = 'jnt:page';
                $('#searchNodeType').val(nodeType);
            }
            nodeType = nodeType.split(":")[1];
            var property = 'hide';
            var defaultSort = 'property';
            switch (nodeType) {
                case 'newsFilterable':
                    property = "date";
                    break;
                case 'hstdocs':
                    property = "confluenceLastModified";
                    defaultSort = "score";
                    break;
                case 'jwstdocs':
                    property = "confluenceLastModified";
                    defaultSort = "score";
                    break;
                case 'event':
                    property = "startDate";
                    break;
                case 'searchableAnnualReport':
                    property = "mYear";
                    break;
                case 'searchableNewsletterArticle':
                    property = "mYear";
                    break;
                case 'mediaLibraryPressRelease':
                    property = "publicationDate";
                    break;
                case 'mediaLibraryImage':
                    property = "mPublicationDate";
                    break;
                case 'mediaLibraryVideo':
                    property = "mPublicationDate";
                    break;
            }
            if (property == 'hide') {
                $('#searchOrderByContainer').hide();
            }
            else {
                $('#searchOrderByContainer').show();
                $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('value', property);
                $('#searchOrderOperand').attr('value', defaultSort);
                if ( defaultSort == 'score') {
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', false);
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', true);
                }
                else {
                    $('#searchOrderByDate').attr('selected', true);
                    $('#searchOrderByScore').attr('selected', false);
                }
            }
            return property;
        }
        function cleanURL() {
            if (location.href.indexOf('.searchVerifyRecaptcha.do') > -1) {
                var uri = location.protocol + "//" + location.host + location.pathname;
                clean_uri = uri.replace('.searchVerifyRecaptcha.do', '');
                window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, clean_uri);
            }
        }
        $(document).ready(function() {
            cleanURL();
            $('.advanced-search-toggle').click(function() {
                $('#advancedSearch').slideToggle(400);
                showAdvancedHelp();
                $('#searchTerm').focus();
                $("#search-input").attr('autocomplete', 'off');
                searchNodeTypeChange();
                searchOrderByOpen();
            });
            $('#searchMethod').change(showAdvancedHelp);
            $('#searchNodeType').change(searchNodeTypeChange);
            $('#searchOrderBy').change(searchOrderByChange);
        });
  </script>
